<<<FILE ./visualizer/server.go>>>
package visualizer

import (
	"context"
	"encoding/json"
	"errors"
	"fmt"
	"net"
	"net/http"
	"runtime"
	"strconv"
	"sync"
	"time"

	_ "net/http/pprof"

	"github.com/gorilla/websocket"
	"github.com/theapemachine/six/pkg/errnie"
	"github.com/theapemachine/six/pkg/system/pool"
	"github.com/theapemachine/six/pkg/telemetry"
)

/*
PromptFunc is the callback signature for handling prompts from the UI.
*/
type PromptFunc func(msg string) ([]byte, error)

/*
IngestFunc is the callback signature for ingesting training data from the UI.
*/
type IngestFunc func(raw []byte) error

/*
wsCommand is a JSON message received from a WebSocket client.
*/
type wsCommand struct {
	Type    string `json:"type"`
	Message string `json:"message"`
}

/*
Server serves the 3D visualization and streams value events via WebSocket.
*/
type Server struct {
	state      *errnie.State
	mu         sync.RWMutex
	clients    map[*websocket.Conn]bool
	upgrade    websocket.Upgrader
	httpSrv    *http.Server
	udpConn    *net.UDPConn
	pool       *pool.Pool
	promptFunc PromptFunc
	ingestFunc IngestFunc
}

/*
NewServer instantiates a visualization server.
*/
func NewServer() *Server {
	return &Server{
		state:   errnie.NewState("visualizer/server"),
		clients: make(map[*websocket.Conn]bool),
		upgrade: websocket.Upgrader{
			CheckOrigin: func(r *http.Request) bool { return true },
		},
		pool: pool.New(
			context.Background(),
			1,
			runtime.NumCPU(),
			&pool.Config{},
		),
	}
}

/*
listenUDP starts the locked UDP listener, forwarding all telemetry to visualizer clients.
*/
func (server *Server) listenUDP(conn *net.UDPConn) error {
	buf := make([]byte, 65535)

	for {
		n, _, err := conn.ReadFromUDP(buf)
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		event := telemetry.DecodeBinary(buf[:n])
		server.Broadcast(event)
	}
}

/*
ListenAndServe starts the HTTP server on the given address.
*/
func (server *Server) ListenAndServe(addr string, udpAddr string) error {
	// These 2 lines are only required if you're using mutex or block profiling
	// Read the explanation below for how to set these rates:
	runtime.SetMutexProfileFraction(5)
	runtime.SetBlockProfileRate(5)

	udpListenAddr := errnie.Guard(server.state, func() (*net.UDPAddr, error) {
		return resolveUDPListenAddr(addr, udpAddr)
	})

	if server.state.Failed() {
		return server.state.Err()
	}

	conn := errnie.Guard(server.state, func() (*net.UDPConn, error) {
		return net.ListenUDP("udp", udpListenAddr)
	})

	if server.state.Failed() {
		return server.state.Err()
	}

	server.udpConn = conn

	go func() {
		if err := server.listenUDP(conn); err != nil && !errors.Is(err, net.ErrClosed) {
			server.state.Handle(err)
		}
	}()

	mux := http.NewServeMux()
	mux.Handle("/", http.FileServer(http.Dir("visualizer/static")))
	mux.HandleFunc("/ws", server.handleWS)

	server.httpSrv = &http.Server{Addr: addr, Handler: mux}

	return server.httpSrv.ListenAndServe()
}

/*
resolveUDPListenAddr derives the UDP bind address from the HTTP listen address
unless an explicit UDP address is provided.
*/
func resolveUDPListenAddr(httpAddr string, udpAddr string) (*net.UDPAddr, error) {
	if udpAddr != "" {
		return net.ResolveUDPAddr("udp", udpAddr)
	}

	host, portText, err := net.SplitHostPort(httpAddr)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	if host == "" {
		host = "127.0.0.1"
	}

	port, err := strconv.Atoi(portText)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	return net.ResolveUDPAddr(
		"udp",
		net.JoinHostPort(host, strconv.Itoa(port+1)),
	)
}

/*
Shutdown gracefully stops the HTTP server and UDP listener.
*/
func (server *Server) Shutdown() {
	if server.udpConn != nil {
		server.udpConn.Close()
	}

	if server.httpSrv != nil {
		shutdownCtx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 2*time.Second)
		defer cancel()

		server.httpSrv.Shutdown(shutdownCtx)
	}

	if server.pool != nil {
		server.pool.Close()
	}
}

/*
SetPromptFunc registers the callback invoked when a client sends a prompt.
*/
func (server *Server) SetPromptFunc(fn PromptFunc) {
	server.mu.Lock()
	defer server.mu.Unlock()

	server.promptFunc = fn
}

/*
SetIngestFunc registers the callback invoked when a client sends training data.
*/
func (server *Server) SetIngestFunc(fn IngestFunc) {
	server.mu.Lock()
	defer server.mu.Unlock()

	server.ingestFunc = fn
}

func (server *Server) handleWS(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	conn := errnie.Guard(server.state, func() (*websocket.Conn, error) {
		return server.upgrade.Upgrade(w, r, nil)
	})

	server.mu.Lock()
	server.clients[conn] = true
	server.mu.Unlock()

	defer func() {
		server.mu.Lock()
		delete(server.clients, conn)
		server.mu.Unlock()
		conn.Close()
	}()

	for {
		_, msg, err := conn.ReadMessage()
		if err != nil {
			break
		}

		var cmd wsCommand

		if json.Unmarshal(msg, &cmd) != nil {
			continue
		}

		switch cmd.Type {
		case "prompt":
			if cmd.Message != "" {
				server.handlePromptCommand(cmd.Message)
			}
		case "ingest":
			if cmd.Message != "" {
				server.handleIngestCommand(cmd.Message)
			}
		}
	}
}

func (server *Server) handlePromptCommand(msg string) {
	server.mu.RLock()
	fn := server.promptFunc
	server.mu.RUnlock()

	if fn == nil {
		server.Broadcast(telemetry.Event{
			Component: "Machine",
			Action:    "Pipeline",
			Data: telemetry.EventData{
				Stage:   "prompt-error",
				Message: "no machine connected",
			},
		})

		return
	}

	result, err := fn(msg)

	if err != nil {
		server.Broadcast(telemetry.Event{
			Component: "Machine",
			Action:    "Pipeline",
			Data: telemetry.EventData{
				Stage:   "prompt-error",
				Message: err.Error(),
			},
		})

		return
	}

	_ = result
}

func (server *Server) handleIngestCommand(text string) {
	server.mu.RLock()
	fn := server.ingestFunc
	server.mu.RUnlock()

	if fn == nil {
		server.Broadcast(telemetry.Event{
			Component: "Machine",
			Action:    "Pipeline",
			Data: telemetry.EventData{
				Stage:   "ingest-error",
				Message: "no machine connected",
			},
		})

		return
	}

	server.Broadcast(telemetry.Event{
		Component: "Machine",
		Action:    "Pipeline",
		Data: telemetry.EventData{
			Stage:   "ingest-start",
			Message: fmt.Sprintf("%d bytes", len(text)),
		},
	})

	if err := fn([]byte(text)); err != nil {
		server.Broadcast(telemetry.Event{
			Component: "Machine",
			Action:    "Pipeline",
			Data: telemetry.EventData{
				Stage:   "ingest-error",
				Message: err.Error(),
			},
		})

		return
	}

	server.Broadcast(telemetry.Event{
		Component: "Machine",
		Action:    "Pipeline",
		Data: telemetry.EventData{
			Stage:   "ingest-complete",
			Message: fmt.Sprintf("%d bytes ingested", len(text)),
		},
	})
}

/*
Broadcast sends an event to all connected WebSocket clients.
*/
func (server *Server) Broadcast(event telemetry.Event) {
	msg := errnie.Guard(server.state, func() ([]byte, error) {
		return json.Marshal(event)
	})

	server.mu.RLock()
	defer server.mu.RUnlock()

	for conn := range server.clients {
		conn.WriteMessage(websocket.TextMessage, msg)
	}
}

      content: attr(data-label);

    /* ── Zone Glow (hover feedback on 3D zones) ──────────── */
    @keyframes zone-glow-pulse {
      0%, 100% { opacity: 0.06; }
      50% { opacity: 0.18; }
    }

  <div id="replay-bar" class="panel">
    <button id="btn-mode-fold" class="graph-mode-btn" title="Fold graph only">Fold</button>

    <button id="btn-play" title="Play recorded events">▶</button>
    <button id="btn-pause" title="Pause">⏸</button>
    <button id="btn-step" title="Step forward">⏭</button>
    <input type="range" id="replay-slider" min="0" max="0" value="0" step="1">
    <span id="replay-info">0 / 0</span>
    <button id="btn-export" title="Export JSON">⬇</button>
    <button id="btn-import" title="Import JSON">⬆</button>
    <input type="file" id="import-file" accept=".json" style="display:none">
  </div>

  <script type="importmap">
    { "imports": { "three": "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/three@0.163.0/build/three.module.js", "three/addons/": "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/three@0.163.0/examples/jsm/" } }
  </script>

  <script type="module">
    import * as THREE from 'three';
    import { OrbitControls } from 'three/addons/controls/OrbitControls.js';
    import { CSS2DRenderer, CSS2DObject } from 'three/addons/renderers/CSS2DRenderer.js';

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // RECORDING / REPLAY ENGINE
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const recording = [];
    let replayMode = false;
    let replayIdx = 0;
    let replayTimer = null;
    const startTime = Date.now();

    function recordEvent(ev) {
      ev._ts = Date.now() - startTime;
      recording.push(ev);
      slider.max = recording.length - 1;
      replayInfo.textContent = `${recording.length} events`;
      statEvents.textContent = recording.length;
    }

    function enterReplayMode() {
      replayMode = true;
      statReplay.textContent = 'replay';
      statReplay.style.color = 'rgba(255, 220, 140, 0.8)';
      btnRec.classList.remove('active');
      resetVisualization();
    }

    function enterLiveMode() {
      replayMode = false;
      if (replayTimer) { clearInterval(replayTimer); replayTimer = null; }
      statReplay.textContent = 'live';
      statReplay.style.color = 'rgba(140, 255, 200, 0.75)';
      btnRec.classList.add('active');
    }

    function replayTo(idx) {
      resetVisualization();
      const target = Math.min(idx, recording.length - 1);
      for (let i = 0; i <= target; i++) handleEvent(recording[i]);
      replayIdx = target;
      slider.value = replayIdx;
      replayInfo.textContent = `${replayIdx + 1} / ${recording.length}`;
    }

    function startPlayback() {
      enterReplayMode();
      if (replayTimer) clearInterval(replayTimer);
      replayTimer = setInterval(() => {
        if (replayIdx < recording.length - 1) {
          replayIdx++;
          handleEvent(recording[replayIdx]);
          slider.value = replayIdx;
          replayInfo.textContent = `${replayIdx + 1} / ${recording.length}`;
        } else {
          clearInterval(replayTimer);
          replayTimer = null;
        }
      }, 16);
    }

    function pausePlayback() {
      if (replayTimer) { clearInterval(replayTimer); replayTimer = null; }
    }

    function stepForward() {
      if (!replayMode) enterReplayMode();
      if (replayIdx < recording.length - 1) {
        replayIdx++;
        handleEvent(recording[replayIdx]);
        slider.value = replayIdx;
        replayInfo.textContent = `${replayIdx + 1} / ${recording.length}`;
      }
    }

    function exportRecording() {
      const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(recording, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
      const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      const a = document.createElement('a');
      a.href = url;
      a.download = `six-recording-${new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-')}.json`;
      a.click();
      URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    }

    function importRecording(file) {
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = (e) => {
        try {
          const data = JSON.parse(e.target.result);
          if (Array.isArray(data)) {
            recording.length = 0;
            recording.push(...data);
            slider.max = recording.length - 1;
            replayInfo.textContent = `${recording.length} events`;
            statEvents.textContent = recording.length;
            log(`Loaded ${recording.length} events`, 'state');
            replayTo(0);
          }
        } catch (err) {
          console.error('Import error:', err);
        }
      };
      reader.readAsText(file);
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // THREE.JS SCENE
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const scene = new THREE.Scene();

    const camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(55, innerWidth / innerHeight, 0.1, 500);
    camera.position.set(0, 34, 30);

    const renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true, canvas: document.getElementById('three-canvas') || undefined });
    renderer.setSize(innerWidth, innerHeight);
    renderer.setPixelRatio(Math.min(devicePixelRatio, 1.5));
    renderer.setClearColor(0x091428);
    if (!document.getElementById('three-canvas')) {
      renderer.domElement.id = 'three-canvas';
      document.body.insertBefore(renderer.domElement, document.body.firstChild);
    }

    const labelRenderer = new CSS2DRenderer();
    labelRenderer.setSize(innerWidth, innerHeight);
    labelRenderer.domElement.style.position = 'absolute';
    labelRenderer.domElement.style.top = '0';
    labelRenderer.domElement.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
    labelRenderer.domElement.style.zIndex = '1';
    document.body.appendChild(labelRenderer.domElement);

    const controls = new OrbitControls(camera, renderer.domElement);
    controls.enableDamping = true;
    controls.dampingFactor = 0.05;
    controls.target.set(0, 0, 2);

    // ── Lighting ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    scene.add(new THREE.AmbientLight(0x1a3050, 1.2));
    const dirLight = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0x4a80c0, 0.4);
    dirLight.position.set(10, 30, 15);
    scene.add(dirLight);

    // ── Grid ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const gridHelper = new THREE.GridHelper(60, 60, 0x1a3a60, 0x0e2244);
    gridHelper.material.transparent = true;
    gridHelper.material.opacity = 0.25;
    scene.add(gridHelper);

    const gridMajor = new THREE.GridHelper(60, 12, 0x2a5080, 0x2a5080);
    gridMajor.material.transparent = true;
    gridMajor.material.opacity = 0.12;
    gridMajor.position.y = 0.01;
    scene.add(gridMajor);

    // ── Axis Lines ────────────────────────────────────────────
    const axisMat = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({ color: 0x3060a0, transparent: true, opacity: 0.15 });
    for (const [a, b] of [[[-30, 0, 0], [30, 0, 0]], [[0, 0, -20], [0, 0, 20]]]) {
      const g = new THREE.BufferGeometry().setFromPoints([new THREE.Vector3(...a), new THREE.Vector3(...b)]);
      scene.add(new THREE.Line(g, axisMat));
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // SUBSYSTEM ARCHITECTURE
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const zoneGroup = new THREE.Group();
    scene.add(zoneGroup);
    const foldLayer = new THREE.Group();
    scene.add(foldLayer);
    const flowLayer = new THREE.Group();
    scene.add(flowLayer);

    const SYS = {
      machine:   { x: 0,   z: 0,   w: 8, h: 6, label: 'MACHINE',     accent: true },
      dataset:   { x: -16, z: 12,  w: 7, h: 5, label: 'DATASET'              },
      tokenizer: { x: 0,   z: 12,  w: 8, h: 5, label: 'TOKENIZER'            },
      forest:    { x: 16,  z: 12,  w: 7, h: 5, label: 'FOREST · DMT'         },
      graph:     { x: 14,  z: 0,   w: 8, h: 6, label: 'GRAPH'                },
      has:       { x: -14, z: 0,   w: 7, h: 5, label: 'HAS'                  },
      macroIdx:  { x: 0,   z: -12, w: 8, h: 5, label: 'MACRO INDEX'          },
    };

    const CONNS = [
      { from: 'dataset',   to: 'tokenizer', tag: 'raw bytes'   },
      { from: 'tokenizer', to: 'machine',   tag: 'morton keys' },
      { from: 'machine',   to: 'forest',    tag: 'write keys'  },
      { from: 'machine',   to: 'graph',     tag: 'paths'       },
      { from: 'machine',   to: 'has',       tag: 'boundaries'  },
      { from: 'has',       to: 'macroIdx',  tag: 'opcodes'     },
      { from: 'graph',     to: 'macroIdx',  tag: 'tools'       },
      { from: 'graph',     to: 'forest',    tag: 'lookup'      },
    ];

    const zoneMat = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({ color: 0x4080c0, transparent: true, opacity: 0.22 });
    const zoneAccentMat = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({ color: 0xffdc8c, transparent: true, opacity: 0.3 });
    const cornerMat = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({ color: 0x4080c0, transparent: true, opacity: 0.3 });
    const cornerAccentMat = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({ color: 0xffdc8c, transparent: true, opacity: 0.45 });

    for (const [key, sys] of Object.entries(SYS)) {
      const hw = sys.w / 2, hh = sys.h / 2;
      const y = 0.05;
      const corners = [
        new THREE.Vector3(sys.x - hw, y, sys.z - hh),
        new THREE.Vector3(sys.x + hw, y, sys.z - hh),
        new THREE.Vector3(sys.x + hw, y, sys.z + hh),
        new THREE.Vector3(sys.x - hw, y, sys.z + hh),
        new THREE.Vector3(sys.x - hw, y, sys.z - hh),
      ];

      const geo = new THREE.BufferGeometry().setFromPoints(corners);
      zoneGroup.add(new THREE.Line(geo, sys.accent ? zoneAccentMat : zoneMat));

      const cMat = sys.accent ? cornerAccentMat : cornerMat;
      const cs = 0.4;
      for (const c of corners.slice(0, 4)) {
        const hg = new THREE.BufferGeometry().setFromPoints([
          new THREE.Vector3(c.x - cs, y, c.z), new THREE.Vector3(c.x + cs, y, c.z),
        ]);
        zoneGroup.add(new THREE.Line(hg, cMat));

        const vg = new THREE.BufferGeometry().setFromPoints([
          new THREE.Vector3(c.x, y, c.z - cs), new THREE.Vector3(c.x, y, c.z + cs),
        ]);
        zoneGroup.add(new THREE.Line(vg, cMat));
      }

      const div = document.createElement('div');
      div.className = sys.accent ? 'subsystem-label center' : 'subsystem-label';
      div.textContent = sys.label;
      const lbl = new CSS2DObject(div);
      lbl.position.set(sys.x, 0.1, sys.z - hh - 0.8);
      zoneGroup.add(lbl);

      sys.center = new THREE.Vector3(sys.x, 0.3, sys.z);
      sys.labelObj = lbl;
      sys.activeGlow = null;
      sys.glowPlane = null;
    }

    // ── Clickable Zone Planes (invisible, for raycasting) ──
    const zonePlanes = {};
    const raycaster = new THREE.Raycaster();
    const mouseVec = new THREE.Vector2();
    const glowPlaneMat = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({
      color: 0x4080c0, transparent: true, opacity: 0.0, side: THREE.DoubleSide,
    });
    const glowPlaneAccentMat = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({
      color: 0xffdc8c, transparent: true, opacity: 0.0, side: THREE.DoubleSide,
    });

    for (const [key, sys] of Object.entries(SYS)) {
      const planeGeo = new THREE.PlaneGeometry(sys.w, sys.h);
      const mat = (sys.accent ? glowPlaneAccentMat : glowPlaneMat).clone();
      const plane = new THREE.Mesh(planeGeo, mat);
      plane.rotation.x = -Math.PI / 2;
      plane.position.set(sys.x, 0.06, sys.z);
      plane.userData = { sysKey: key };
      scene.add(plane);
      zonePlanes[key] = plane;
      sys.glowPlane = plane;
    }

    // ── Connection Lines ──────────────────────────────────────
    const connDashMat = new THREE.LineDashedMaterial({
      color: 0x3060a0, transparent: true, opacity: 0.14,
      dashSize: 0.6, gapSize: 0.35,
    });

    for (const conn of CONNS) {
      const fromSys = SYS[conn.from], toSys = SYS[conn.to];
      const fromPt = new THREE.Vector3(fromSys.x, 0.04, fromSys.z);
      const toPt = new THREE.Vector3(toSys.x, 0.04, toSys.z);

      const geo = new THREE.BufferGeometry().setFromPoints([fromPt, toPt]);
      const line = new THREE.Line(geo, connDashMat);
      line.computeLineDistances();
      zoneGroup.add(line);

      const mid = new THREE.Vector3().lerpVectors(fromPt, toPt, 0.5);
      const tagDiv = document.createElement('div');
      tagDiv.className = 'conn-label';
      tagDiv.textContent = conn.tag;
      const tagLbl = new CSS2DObject(tagDiv);
      tagLbl.position.copy(mid).setY(0.08);
      zoneGroup.add(tagLbl);

      conn.fromPt = fromPt;
      conn.toPt = toPt;
    }

    // ── Directional Arrows ────────────────────────────────────
    const arrowGeo = new THREE.ConeGeometry(0.18, 0.5, 4);
    const arrowMat = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x3060a0, transparent: true, opacity: 0.2 });

    for (const conn of CONNS) {
      const dir = new THREE.Vector3().subVectors(conn.toPt, conn.fromPt);
      const mid = new THREE.Vector3().lerpVectors(conn.fromPt, conn.toPt, 0.65);

      const arrow = new THREE.Mesh(arrowGeo, arrowMat);
      arrow.position.copy(mid).setY(0.15);
      arrow.quaternion.setFromUnitVectors(
        new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0),
        dir.clone().setY(0).normalize(),
      );
      zoneGroup.add(arrow);
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // DATA STREAMS (text labels flowing between subsystems)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const dataStreams = [];
    const MAX_STREAMS = 60;

    function spawnDataStream(fromKey, toKey, text, streamClass = '', duration = 2800) {
      const from = SYS[fromKey], to = SYS[toKey];
      if (!from || !to) return;

      const displayText = (text || '').trim().slice(0, 32) || '·';
      const pathKey = `${fromKey}>${toKey}`;

      const existing = dataStreams.filter(s => s.pathKey === pathKey);
      if (existing.length > 0) {
        const newest = existing[existing.length - 1];
        const age = (Date.now() - newest.t0) / newest.dur;
        if (age < 0.12) return;
      }

      const div = document.createElement('div');
      div.className = `data-stream-label ${streamClass}`;
      div.textContent = displayText;

      const lbl = new CSS2DObject(div);
      const startPos = from.center.clone().setY(0.12);
      const endPos = to.center.clone().setY(0.12);
      lbl.position.copy(startPos);
      flowLayer.add(lbl);

      dataStreams.push({
        lbl,
        div,
        pathKey,
        start: startPos,
        end: endPos,
        t0: Date.now(),
        dur: duration,
      });

      while (dataStreams.length > MAX_STREAMS) {
        const old = dataStreams.shift();
        flowLayer.remove(old.lbl);
      }
    }

    function updateDataStreams() {
      const now = Date.now();

      for (let i = dataStreams.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        const s = dataStreams[i];
        const t = (now - s.t0) / s.dur;

        if (t >= 1) {
          flowLayer.remove(s.lbl);
          dataStreams.splice(i, 1);
          continue;
        }

        s.lbl.position.lerpVectors(s.start, s.end, t);
        s.div.style.opacity = t < 0.1
          ? (t / 0.1).toFixed(2)
          : t > 0.85
            ? ((1 - t) / 0.15).toFixed(2)
            : '1';
      }
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // ZONE ACTIVITY LABELS (vertical stack, no overlap)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const zoneLabels = new Map();
    const MAX_ZONE_LABELS = 5;
    const ZONE_LABEL_SPACING = 0.55;

    function addZoneLabel(sysKey, text) {
      const sys = SYS[sysKey];
      if (!sys) return;

      const displayText = (text || '').trim().slice(0, 28) || '·';
      const arr = zoneLabels.get(sysKey) || [];

      for (const item of arr) {
        item.div.classList.remove('fresh');
        item.div.classList.add('fading');
      }

      const div = document.createElement('div');
      div.className = 'zone-activity-label fresh';
      div.textContent = displayText;

      const lbl = new CSS2DObject(div);
      zoneGroup.add(lbl);
      arr.push({ lbl, div, time: Date.now() });

      while (arr.length > MAX_ZONE_LABELS) {
        const old = arr.shift();
        zoneGroup.remove(old.lbl);
      }

      const hw = sys.w / 2;
      for (let i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
        const slot = arr.length - 1 - i;
        arr[i].lbl.position.set(
          sys.x - hw + 0.3,
          0.15,
          sys.z + slot * ZONE_LABEL_SPACING - 0.5,
        );
      }

      zoneLabels.set(sysKey, arr);
    }

    function clearZoneLabels(sysKey) {
      const arr = zoneLabels.get(sysKey);
      if (!arr) return;

      for (const item of arr) zoneGroup.remove(item.lbl);
      arr.length = 0;
    }

    function clearAllZoneLabels() {
      for (const [key] of zoneLabels) clearZoneLabels(key);
      zoneLabels.clear();
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // FOLD TREE (within Graph zone, proper tree layout)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const foldNodes = [];
    const foldLevelCounts = {};
    const MAX_FOLD_NODES = 30;
    const foldLineMats = {
      0: new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({ color: 0x6090c0, transparent: true, opacity: 0.3 }),
      1: new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({ color: 0x5080b0, transparent: true, opacity: 0.22 }),
      deep: new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({ color: 0x4070a0, transparent: true, opacity: 0.15 }),
    };

    function addFoldNode(bin, level, density, text, childCount) {
      const sys = SYS.graph;
      const rawText = (text || '').trim();

      foldLevelCounts[level] = (foldLevelCounts[level] || 0) + 1;
      const indexInLevel = foldLevelCounts[level] - 1;

      const levelSpread = sys.w * 0.8;
      const maxPerLevel = Math.max(3, 6 - level);
      const slot = indexInLevel % maxPerLevel;
      const xOffset = (slot - (maxPerLevel - 1) / 2) * (levelSpread / maxPerLevel);

      const x = sys.x + xOffset;
      const y = 0.5 + level * 2.2;
      const z = sys.z + 0.5;

      const levelClass = level === 0 ? 'level-0' : level === 1 ? 'level-1' : level === 2 ? 'level-2' : 'level-deep';
      const div = document.createElement('div');
      div.className = `fold-label ${levelClass}`;

      const textSpan = document.createElement('span');
      textSpan.className = 'fold-text';
      textSpan.textContent = rawText || '[empty]';
      div.appendChild(textSpan);

      const metaSpan = document.createElement('span');
      metaSpan.className = 'fold-meta';
      metaSpan.textContent = `L${level} bin=${bin} ${(density * 100).toFixed(0)}% ch=${childCount || 0}`;
      div.appendChild(metaSpan);

      const lbl = new CSS2DObject(div);
      lbl.position.set(x, y, z);
      foldLayer.add(lbl);

      const pos = new THREE.Vector3(x, y, z);
      const node = { lbl, pos, level, bin };

      if (level > 0 && foldNodes.length > 0) {
        const parentLevel = level - 1;
        const parentCandidates = foldNodes.filter(n => n.level === parentLevel);
        const parent = parentCandidates.length > 0
          ? parentCandidates[parentCandidates.length - 1]
          : foldNodes[foldNodes.length - 1];

        const mat = foldLineMats[level] || foldLineMats.deep;
        const lineGeo = new THREE.BufferGeometry().setFromPoints([parent.pos, pos]);
        const line = new THREE.Line(lineGeo, mat);
        foldLayer.add(line);
        node.line = line;
      }

      foldNodes.push(node);

      while (foldNodes.length > MAX_FOLD_NODES) {
        const old = foldNodes.shift();
        foldLayer.remove(old.lbl);
        if (old.line) { foldLayer.remove(old.line); old.line.geometry.dispose(); }
      }
    }

    function clearFoldNodes() {
      for (const n of foldNodes) {
        foldLayer.remove(n.lbl);
        if (n.line) { foldLayer.remove(n.line); n.line.geometry.dispose(); }
      }
      foldNodes.length = 0;
      for (const key of Object.keys(foldLevelCounts)) delete foldLevelCounts[key];
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // GRAPH MODE TOGGLE
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    function setGraphMode(mode) {
      foldLayer.visible = mode === 'fold' || mode === 'both';
      flowLayer.visible = mode === 'flow' || mode === 'both';
      btnModeFold.classList.toggle('active', mode === 'fold');
      btnModeFlow.classList.toggle('active', mode === 'flow');
      btnModeBoth.classList.toggle('active', mode === 'both');
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // VISUALIZATION RESET
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    function resetVisualization() {
      clearAllZoneLabels();
      clearFoldNodes();

      for (const s of dataStreams) {
        flowLayer.remove(s.lbl);
      }
      dataStreams.length = 0;

      sparkData.length = 0;
      drawSparkline();

      totalIngested = 0; totalEdges = 0; totalQueries = 0; totalPaths = 0; totalFolds = 0;
      totalTokenNodes = 0; totalFlowEdges = 0; totalFoldLinks = 0;
      statIngested.textContent = '0';
      statEdges.textContent = '0';
      statGroups.textContent = '0';
      statQueries.textContent = '0';
      statPaths.textContent = '0';
      statFolds.textContent = '0';
      statTokenNodes.textContent = '0';
      statFlowEdges.textContent = '0';
      statFoldLinks.textContent = '0';
      chunkText.textContent = '—';
      resultText.style.display = 'none';
      logBox.innerHTML = '';

      execPanel.style.display = 'none';
      execSteps.innerHTML = '';
      execOutcome.textContent = '';
      execResidueFill.style.width = '0%';
      execInitialResidue = 0;
    }

    function resetFoldGraph() {
      clearFoldNodes();
      totalFoldLinks = 0;
      statFoldLinks.textContent = '0';
      totalFolds = 0;
      statFolds.textContent = '0';
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // HUD REFERENCES
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const logBox = document.getElementById('log-container');
    const statEvents = document.getElementById('stat-events');
    const statIngested = document.getElementById('stat-ingested');
    const statEdges = document.getElementById('stat-edges');
    const statGroups = document.getElementById('stat-groups');
    const statQueries = document.getElementById('stat-queries');
    const statPaths = document.getElementById('stat-paths');
    const statFolds = document.getElementById('stat-folds');
    const statTokenNodes = document.getElementById('stat-token-nodes');
    const statFlowEdges = document.getElementById('stat-flow-edges');
    const statFoldLinks = document.getElementById('stat-fold-links');
    const statConn = document.getElementById('stat-conn');
    const statReplay = document.getElementById('stat-replay');
    const chunkText = document.getElementById('chunk-text');
    const resultText = document.getElementById('result-text');
    const densityFill = document.getElementById('density-fill');

    const slider = document.getElementById('replay-slider');
    const replayInfo = document.getElementById('replay-info');
    const btnRec = document.getElementById('btn-rec');
    const btnModeFold = document.getElementById('btn-mode-fold');
    const btnModeFlow = document.getElementById('btn-mode-flow');
    const btnModeBoth = document.getElementById('btn-mode-both');
    const btnPlay = document.getElementById('btn-play');
    const btnPause = document.getElementById('btn-pause');
    const btnStep = document.getElementById('btn-step');
    const btnExport = document.getElementById('btn-export');
    const btnImport = document.getElementById('btn-import');
    const importFile = document.getElementById('import-file');
    const promptInput = document.getElementById('prompt-input');
    const promptSend = document.getElementById('prompt-send');
    const ingestToggle = document.getElementById('ingest-toggle');
    const ingestPanel = document.getElementById('ingest-panel');
    const ingestText = document.getElementById('ingest-text');
    const ingestSend = document.getElementById('ingest-send');
    const ingestStatus = document.getElementById('ingest-status');

    const execPanel = document.getElementById('execute-panel');
    const execCandidates = document.getElementById('exec-candidates');
    const execMaxSteps = document.getElementById('exec-max-steps');
    const execSteps = document.getElementById('exec-steps');
    const execResidueFill = document.getElementById('exec-residue-fill');
    const execOutcome = document.getElementById('exec-outcome');

    let execInitialResidue = 0;

    let totalIngested = 0;
    let totalEdges = 0;
    let totalQueries = 0;
    let totalPaths = 0;
    let totalFolds = 0;
    let totalTokenNodes = 0;
    let totalFlowEdges = 0;
    let totalFoldLinks = 0;

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // EVENT ACCUMULATOR (per-component event history)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const eventsByComponent = new Map();
    const MAX_COMPONENT_EVENTS = 300;
    const allEvents = [];

    function accumulateEvent(ev) {
      const key = ev.component || 'unknown';

      if (!eventsByComponent.has(key)) {
        eventsByComponent.set(key, []);
      }

      const arr = eventsByComponent.get(key);
      arr.push(ev);

      while (arr.length > MAX_COMPONENT_EVENTS) {
        arr.shift();
      }

      allEvents.push(ev);

      while (allEvents.length > 2000) {
        allEvents.shift();
      }
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // INSPECTOR STATE
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    let inspectorOpen = false;
    let inspectorSysKey = null;
    let inspectorTab = 'feed';
    let inspectorRefreshTimer = null;

    const ZONE_COMPONENTS = {
      machine:   ['Machine', 'Program'],
      dataset:   ['Dataset'],
      tokenizer: ['Tokenizer', 'Sequencer'],
      forest:    ['LSM', 'DMT'],
      graph:     ['Graph', 'SpatialIndex'],
      has:       ['HAS'],
      macroIdx:  ['MacroIndex'],
    };

    const ZONE_DESCRIPTIONS = {
      machine:   'Central orchestrator — pipeline, execution, coordination',
      dataset:   'External data source — raw byte streams',
      tokenizer: 'Byte-level sequencer — boundary detection, morton coding',
      forest:    'Immutable radix trie — key-value storage, prefix search',
      graph:     'Logic substrate — recursive folding, AST graph, evaluation',
      has:       'Boundary detection — affine derivation, pressure signals',
      macroIdx:  'Opcode registry — macro instructions, candidate tracking',
    };

    const inspectorPanel = document.getElementById('inspector-panel');
    const inspectorTitle = document.getElementById('inspector-title');
    const inspectorDesc = document.getElementById('inspector-desc');
    const inspectorBody = document.getElementById('inspector-body');
    const inspectorCloseBtn = document.getElementById('inspector-close');
    const inspectorTabsEl = document.getElementById('inspector-tabs');
    const eventDetailOverlay = document.getElementById('event-detail-overlay');
    const eventDetailJson = document.getElementById('event-detail-json');
    const eventDetailCloseBtn = document.getElementById('event-detail-close');
    const logSearch = document.getElementById('log-search');

    // Accumulated data for subsystem-specific visualizations
    const forestKeyBins = new Uint32Array(256);
    let forestEntryCount = 0;
    const tokenBinCounts = new Uint32Array(256);
    let tokenBinMax = 1;
    const promptHistory = [];
    const foldHistory = [];
    const executeHistory = [];

    function log(text, type = 'state', eventRef = null) {
      const div = document.createElement('div');
      div.className = `log-line log-${type}`;
      div.dataset.type = type;
      const t = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[1].slice(0, -1);
      div.textContent = `${t} ${text}`;

      if (eventRef) {
        div._eventRef = eventRef;
        div.addEventListener('click', () => showEventDetail(eventRef));
      }

      logBox.insertBefore(div, logBox.firstChild);

      while (logBox.children.length > 80) {
        logBox.removeChild(logBox.lastChild);
      }

      applyLogFilters();
    }

    // ── Pipeline Stage Management ────────────────────────────
    const stageElements = {
      'tokenize': document.getElementById('stage-tokenize'),
      'insert': document.getElementById('stage-insert'),
      'lookup': document.getElementById('stage-lookup'),
      'fold': document.getElementById('stage-fold'),
      'decode': document.getElementById('stage-decode'),
    };
    const stageInfoElements = {
      'tokenize': document.getElementById('stage-tokenize-info'),
      'insert': document.getElementById('stage-insert-info'),
      'lookup': document.getElementById('stage-lookup-info'),
      'fold': document.getElementById('stage-fold-info'),
      'decode': document.getElementById('stage-decode-info'),
    };

    let clearPipelineTimer = null;

    function activateStage(name, info) {
      for (const el of Object.values(stageElements)) {
        if (el.classList.contains('active')) {
          el.classList.remove('active');
          el.classList.add('done');
        }
      }

      const el = stageElements[name];
      if (el) { el.classList.remove('done'); el.classList.add('active'); }
      if (info && stageInfoElements[name]) stageInfoElements[name].textContent = info;

      if (clearPipelineTimer) clearTimeout(clearPipelineTimer);
      clearPipelineTimer = setTimeout(() => {
        Object.values(stageElements).forEach(el => { el.classList.remove('active', 'done'); });
        Object.values(stageInfoElements).forEach(el => { el.textContent = ''; });
      }, 3000);
    }

    function updateDensityBar(edgeCount) {
      const pct = Math.min((edgeCount / 5000) * 100, 100);
      densityFill.style.height = `${pct * 1.4}px`;
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // EVENT HANDLER (routes to subsystem zones)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    function handleEvent(ev) {
      const d = ev.data || {};

      accumulateEvent(ev);

      if (ev.component === 'DMT' && ev.action === 'Insert') {
        if (d.bin !== undefined) {
          forestKeyBins[d.bin & 0xFF]++;
        }

        if (d.entryCount) {
          forestEntryCount = d.entryCount;
        }

        addZoneLabel('forest', `entry #${d.entryCount || '?'}`);
        refreshInspectorIfMatch('forest');
      }

      if (ev.component === 'Tokenizer' && ev.action === 'Value') {
        const stage = d.stage || '';
        const edgeCount = d.edgeCount || 0;
        const text = d.chunkText || '';

        if (stage === 'ingest-tokenize') {
          totalIngested++;
          statIngested.textContent = totalIngested;
          chunkText.textContent = text.slice(0, 120);
          activateStage('tokenize', `${edgeCount} edges`);

          spawnDataStream('dataset', 'tokenizer', text || 'raw bytes', 'stream-ingest', 1200);
          addZoneLabel('tokenizer', text);
          log(`Ingest: "${text.slice(0, 50)}"`, 'ingest', ev);
        }

        if (stage === 'tokenize') {
          totalQueries++;
          statQueries.textContent = totalQueries;
          activateStage('tokenize', `${edgeCount} edges`);

          spawnDataStream('tokenizer', 'machine', text || 'tokens', 'stream-token', 1000);
          addZoneLabel('tokenizer', text);
          log(`Query: "${text.slice(0, 50)}"`, 'tokenize', ev);
        }

        if (d.bin !== undefined) {
          totalTokenNodes++;
          statTokenNodes.textContent = totalTokenNodes;
          statGroups.textContent = Math.min(totalTokenNodes, 256);
          tokenBinCounts[d.bin & 0xFF]++;
          tokenBinMax = Math.max(tokenBinMax, tokenBinCounts[d.bin & 0xFF]);
        }

        refreshInspectorIfMatch('tokenizer');
      }

      else if (ev.component === 'LSM' && ev.action === 'Insert') {
        const edges = d.edges || d.edgeCount || 0;
        const insertText = d.chunkText || `${edges} edge`;
        totalEdges += edges;
        statEdges.textContent = totalEdges;
        activateStage('insert', `${edges} stored`);
        updateDensityBar(totalEdges);

        spawnDataStream('machine', 'forest', insertText, 'stream-store', 1400);
        totalFlowEdges++;
        statFlowEdges.textContent = totalFlowEdges;
        log(`Radix insert: ${insertText}`, 'ingest', ev);
        refreshInspectorIfMatch('forest');
      }

      else if (ev.component === 'SpatialIndex' && ev.action === 'Lookup') {
        const pathCount = d.pathCount || d.paths || 0;
        totalPaths += pathCount;
        statPaths.textContent = totalPaths;
        activateStage('lookup', `${pathCount} paths`);

        spawnDataStream('graph', 'machine', `${pathCount} paths found`, 'stream-lookup', 1000);
        addZoneLabel('graph', `${pathCount} paths`);
        log(`Lookup: ${pathCount} paths`, 'lookup', ev);
        refreshInspectorIfMatch('graph');
      }

      else if (ev.component === 'Graph' && ev.action === 'Evaluate') {
        const pathCount = d.pathCount || 0;
        activateStage('fold', `${pathCount} results`);

        spawnDataStream('machine', 'graph', `evaluate ${pathCount} paths`, 'stream-fold', 1200);
        log(`Fold complete: ${pathCount} result paths`, 'fold', ev);
        refreshInspectorIfMatch('graph');
      }

      else if (ev.component === 'Graph' && ev.action === 'Fold') {
        totalFolds++;
        statFolds.textContent = totalFolds;
        totalFoldLinks++;
        statFoldLinks.textContent = totalFoldLinks;

        const foldText = d.chunkText || '';
        addFoldNode(d.bin || 0, d.level || 0, d.density || 0, foldText, d.childCount || 0);
        spawnDataStream('graph', 'macroIdx', foldText || `L${d.level} fold`, 'stream-fold', 1400);
        foldHistory.push({ level: d.level || 0, bin: d.bin || 0, density: d.density || 0, text: foldText, children: d.childCount || 0, ts: ev._ts });
        while (foldHistory.length > 200) foldHistory.shift();
        log(`Fold L${d.level} bin=${d.bin} children=${d.childCount} "${foldText.slice(0, 40)}"`, 'fold', ev);
        refreshInspectorIfMatch('graph');
      }

      else if (ev.component === 'Machine' && ev.action === 'Pipeline') {
        const stage = d.stage || '';

        if (stage === 'prompt-start') {
          resetFoldGraph();
          clearZoneLabels('graph');
          const promptText = d.message || d.msg || '';
          chunkText.textContent = `Query: ${promptText}`;
          resultText.style.display = 'none';
          for (const el of Object.values(stageElements)) el.classList.remove('active', 'done');

          spawnDataStream('dataset', 'tokenizer', promptText, 'stream-prompt', 800);
          setTimeout(() => spawnDataStream('tokenizer', 'machine', promptText, 'stream-prompt', 800), 400);
          setTimeout(() => {
            spawnDataStream('machine', 'graph', promptText, 'stream-prompt', 800);
            spawnDataStream('machine', 'has', promptText, 'stream-prompt', 900);
          }, 800);

          addZoneLabel('machine', promptText);
          promptHistory.push({ prompt: promptText, result: null, error: null, ts: ev._ts, stage: 'pending' });
          while (promptHistory.length > 50) promptHistory.shift();
          log(`Prompt: "${promptText.slice(0, 50)}"`, 'pipeline', ev);
        }

        if (stage === 'prompt-complete') {
          activateStage('decode', '✓');
          const resultContent = (d.resultText || '').slice(0, 200);
          resultText.textContent = `Result: ${resultContent}`;
          resultText.style.display = 'block';

          spawnDataStream('graph', 'machine', resultContent || 'result', 'stream-result', 1000);
          addZoneLabel('machine', resultContent.slice(0, 30));

          const lastPrompt = promptHistory[promptHistory.length - 1];
          if (lastPrompt) { lastPrompt.result = resultContent; lastPrompt.stage = 'complete'; }

          log(`Result: "${resultContent.slice(0, 60)}"`, 'result', ev);
        }

        if (stage === 'prompt-empty') {
          activateStage('decode', '∅');
          resultText.textContent = 'No result';
          resultText.style.display = 'block';

          const lastPrompt = promptHistory[promptHistory.length - 1];
          if (lastPrompt) { lastPrompt.result = '∅ empty'; lastPrompt.stage = 'empty'; }

          log(`Empty result`, 'state', ev);
        }

        if (stage === 'prompt-error') {
          resultText.textContent = `Error: ${d.message || 'unknown'}`;
          resultText.style.display = 'block';
          resultText.style.color = 'var(--bp-red)';

          const lastPrompt = promptHistory[promptHistory.length - 1];
          if (lastPrompt) { lastPrompt.error = d.message; lastPrompt.stage = 'error'; }

          log(`Prompt error: ${d.message}`, 'state', ev);
        }

        refreshInspectorIfMatch('machine');

        if (stage === 'ingest-start') {
          ingestStatus.textContent = `ingesting ${d.message}…`;
          ingestStatus.style.color = 'var(--bp-ink-dim)';
          log(`Ingest started: ${d.message}`, 'pipeline');
        }

        if (stage === 'ingest-complete') {
          ingestStatus.textContent = d.message;
          ingestStatus.style.color = 'var(--bp-green)';
          ingestSend.disabled = false;
          ingestText.value = '';
          log(`Ingest complete: ${d.message}`, 'pipeline');
        }

        if (stage === 'ingest-error') {
          ingestStatus.textContent = `Error: ${d.message}`;
          ingestStatus.style.color = 'var(--bp-red)';
          ingestSend.disabled = false;
          log(`Ingest error: ${d.message}`, 'state');
        }
      }

      else if (ev.component === 'Sequencer' && ev.action === 'Boundary') {
        const densityPct = ((d.density || 0) * 100).toFixed(0);
        spawnDataStream('tokenizer', 'machine', `chunk #${d.chunks} ${densityPct}%`, 'stream-token', 800);
        log(`Boundary #${d.chunks} density=${((d.density || 0) * 100).toFixed(1)}%`, 'tokenize');
      }

      else if (ev.component === 'Program' && ev.action === 'Execute') {
        const stage = d.stage || '';

        if (stage === 'start') {
          execPanel.style.display = 'block';
          execCandidates.textContent = d.candidateCount || 0;
          execMaxSteps.textContent = d.maxSteps || 0;
          execSteps.innerHTML = '';
          execOutcome.textContent = '';
          execOutcome.className = 'exec-outcome';
          execInitialResidue = d.preResidue || 1;
          execResidueFill.style.width = '100%';

          spawnDataStream('machine', 'graph', `${d.candidateCount} candidates`, 'stream-prompt', 1000);
          addZoneLabel('machine', `Execute: ${d.candidateCount} candidates`);
          executeHistory.push({ stage: 'start', candidates: d.candidateCount, preResidue: d.preResidue, steps: [], ts: ev._ts });
          while (executeHistory.length > 30) executeHistory.shift();
          log(`Execute start: residue=${d.preResidue} candidates=${d.candidateCount}`, 'pipeline', ev);
        }

        if (stage === 'step') {
          const step = d.step || 0;
          const pre = d.preResidue || 0;
          const post = d.postResidue || 0;
          const adv = d.advanced;
          const stb = d.stable;

          const cls = stb ? 'stable' : adv ? 'advanced' : 'stalled';
          const row = document.createElement('div');
          row.className = `exec-step ${cls}`;
          row.textContent = `step ${step}: ${pre} → ${post}${stb ? ' ✓' : adv ? ' ↓' : ' ✗'}`;
          execSteps.appendChild(row);
          execSteps.scrollTop = execSteps.scrollHeight;

          const pct = execInitialResidue > 0
            ? Math.max(0, post / execInitialResidue) * 100
            : 0;
          execResidueFill.style.width = `${pct}%`;

          const stepLabel = `step ${step}: ${pre}→${post}`;
          spawnDataStream('machine', 'graph', stepLabel, adv ? 'stream-result' : 'stream-fold', 700);

          const lastExec = executeHistory[executeHistory.length - 1];
          if (lastExec) lastExec.steps.push({ step, pre, post, advanced: adv, stable: stb });

          log(`Execute step ${step}: ${pre}→${post} ${cls}`, 'pipeline', ev);
        }

        if (stage === 'complete') {
          const outcome = d.outcome || '';
          execOutcome.textContent = outcome;
          execOutcome.className = `exec-outcome ${outcome}`;

          if (outcome === 'stable') {
            execResidueFill.style.width = '0%';
            spawnDataStream('graph', 'machine', `stable (step ${d.step})`, 'stream-result', 1000);
          }

          const lastExec = executeHistory[executeHistory.length - 1];
          if (lastExec) { lastExec.outcome = outcome; lastExec.finalStep = d.step; lastExec.postResidue = d.postResidue; }

          addZoneLabel('machine', `Execute: ${outcome} (step ${d.step})`);
          log(`Execute ${outcome}: step=${d.step} residue=${d.postResidue}`, 'pipeline', ev);
        }

        refreshInspectorIfMatch('machine');
      }

      else if (ev.component === 'Graph' && ev.action === 'FoldSpan') {
        const level = d.level || 0;
        const spanSize = d.spanSize || 0;
        const spanText = d.chunkText || '';
        const spanLabel = spanText
          ? `"${spanText.slice(0, 20)}" L${level} [${d.left}:${d.right}]`
          : `L${level} [${d.left}:${d.right}] ×${spanSize}`;

        addZoneLabel('graph', spanLabel);
        log(`FoldSpan L${level}: [${d.left}:${d.right}] "${spanText.slice(0, 40)}"`, 'fold');

        if (level === 0) {
          spawnDataStream('machine', 'graph', spanText || `span [${d.left}:${d.right}]`, 'stream-fold', 1000);
        }
      }

      else if (ev.component === 'Chaos') {
        const density = d.density || 0;
        pushSparkDensity(density, ev.action || '');
        log(`${ev.action}: [${(d.activeBits || []).length} bits, ${(density * 100).toFixed(1)}%]`, 'fold');

        if (density > 0) {
          densityFill.style.height = `${Math.min(density * 100, 100) * 1.4}px`;
        }
      }
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // WEBSOCKET
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    let activeWS = null;

    function connect() {
      const ws = new WebSocket(`ws://${location.host}/ws`);

      ws.onopen = () => {
        activeWS = ws;
        statConn.textContent = 'connected';
        statConn.style.color = 'rgba(140, 255, 200, 0.75)';
        promptSend.disabled = false;
        log('Connected to SIX telemetry', 'state');
      };

      ws.onclose = () => {
        activeWS = null;
        statConn.textContent = 'offline';
        statConn.style.color = 'rgba(255, 140, 120, 0.7)';
        promptSend.disabled = true;
        log('Disconnected', 'state');
        setTimeout(connect, 2000);
      };

      ws.onmessage = (event) => {
        try {
          const ev = JSON.parse(event.data);
          recordEvent(ev);
          if (!replayMode) handleEvent(ev);
        } catch (e) {
          console.error('Parse:', e);
        }
      };
    }

    function sendPrompt(msg) {
      if (!activeWS || activeWS.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN || !msg.trim()) return;

      activeWS.send(JSON.stringify({ type: 'prompt', message: msg.trim() }));
      promptInput.value = '';
      promptSend.disabled = true;
      log(`Sent prompt: "${msg.trim()}"`, 'pipeline');

      setTimeout(() => { promptSend.disabled = !activeWS; }, 300);
    }

    function sendIngest(text) {
      if (!activeWS || activeWS.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN || !text.trim()) return;

      ingestSend.disabled = true;
      ingestStatus.textContent = 'ingesting…';
      ingestStatus.style.color = 'var(--bp-ink-dim)';
      activeWS.send(JSON.stringify({ type: 'ingest', message: text }));
      log(`Ingesting ${text.length} bytes`, 'pipeline');
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // REPLAY CONTROLS
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    btnRec.addEventListener('click', enterLiveMode);
    btnModeFold.addEventListener('click', () => setGraphMode('fold'));
    btnModeFlow.addEventListener('click', () => setGraphMode('flow'));
    btnModeBoth.addEventListener('click', () => setGraphMode('both'));
    btnPlay.addEventListener('click', startPlayback);
    btnPause.addEventListener('click', pausePlayback);
    btnStep.addEventListener('click', stepForward);
    btnExport.addEventListener('click', exportRecording);
    btnImport.addEventListener('click', () => importFile.click());
    importFile.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
      if (e.target.files.length) importRecording(e.target.files[0]);
    });

    promptSend.addEventListener('click', () => sendPrompt(promptInput.value));
    promptInput.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
      if (e.key === 'Enter') sendPrompt(promptInput.value);
    });

    ingestToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const open = ingestPanel.classList.toggle('open');
      ingestToggle.textContent = open ? '▾ training data' : '▴ training data';
    });

    ingestSend.addEventListener('click', () => sendIngest(ingestText.value));

    slider.addEventListener('input', () => {
      if (!replayMode) enterReplayMode();
      pausePlayback();
      replayTo(parseInt(slider.value));
    });

    setGraphMode('both');

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // INSPECTOR PANEL (click-to-inspect subsystem zones)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    let mouseDownPos = null;

    renderer.domElement.addEventListener('pointerdown', (e) => {
      mouseDownPos = { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY };
    });

    renderer.domElement.addEventListener('pointerup', (e) => {
      if (!mouseDownPos) return;

      const dx = e.clientX - mouseDownPos.x;
      const dy = e.clientY - mouseDownPos.y;

      if (Math.abs(dx) > 4 || Math.abs(dy) > 4) return;

      mouseVec.x = (e.clientX / innerWidth) * 2 - 1;
      mouseVec.y = -(e.clientY / innerHeight) * 2 + 1;
      raycaster.setFromCamera(mouseVec, camera);

      const planes = Object.values(zonePlanes);
      const hits = raycaster.intersectObjects(planes);

      if (hits.length > 0) {
        openInspector(hits[0].object.userData.sysKey);
      }
    });

    renderer.domElement.addEventListener('pointermove', (e) => {
      mouseVec.x = (e.clientX / innerWidth) * 2 - 1;
      mouseVec.y = -(e.clientY / innerHeight) * 2 + 1;
      raycaster.setFromCamera(mouseVec, camera);

      const planes = Object.values(zonePlanes);
      const hits = raycaster.intersectObjects(planes);

      for (const [key, plane] of Object.entries(zonePlanes)) {
        const isHit = hits.length > 0 && hits[0].object === plane;
        plane.material.opacity = isHit ? 0.08 : 0.0;
      }

      renderer.domElement.style.cursor = hits.length > 0 ? 'pointer' : '';
    });

    function openInspector(sysKey) {
      inspectorSysKey = sysKey;
      inspectorOpen = true;
      inspectorTab = 'feed';

      inspectorPanel.classList.add('open');
      inspectorTitle.textContent = SYS[sysKey]?.label || sysKey;
      inspectorDesc.textContent = ZONE_DESCRIPTIONS[sysKey] || '';

      const tabs = inspectorTabsEl.querySelectorAll('.inspector-tab');
      tabs.forEach(t => t.classList.toggle('active', t.dataset.tab === 'feed'));

      renderInspector();
    }

    function closeInspector() {
      inspectorOpen = false;
      inspectorSysKey = null;
      inspectorPanel.classList.remove('open');
    }

    inspectorCloseBtn.addEventListener('click', closeInspector);

    inspectorTabsEl.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      const tab = e.target.closest('.inspector-tab');
      if (!tab) return;

      inspectorTab = tab.dataset.tab;
      inspectorTabsEl.querySelectorAll('.inspector-tab').forEach(
        t => t.classList.toggle('active', t.dataset.tab === inspectorTab),
      );

      renderInspector();
    });

    function refreshInspectorIfMatch(sysKey) {
      if (!inspectorOpen || inspectorSysKey !== sysKey) return;

      if (inspectorRefreshTimer) return;
      inspectorRefreshTimer = setTimeout(() => {
        inspectorRefreshTimer = null;
        renderInspector();
      }, 200);
    }

    function renderInspector() {
      if (!inspectorOpen || !inspectorSysKey) return;

      if (inspectorTab === 'feed') renderFeedTab();
      else if (inspectorTab === 'state') renderStateTab();
      else if (inspectorTab === 'internals') renderInternalsTab();
    }

    // ── Feed Tab ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    function renderFeedTab() {
      const components = ZONE_COMPONENTS[inspectorSysKey] || [];
      const events = [];

      for (const comp of components) {
        const arr = eventsByComponent.get(comp) || [];
        events.push(...arr);
      }

      events.sort((a, b) => (b._ts || 0) - (a._ts || 0));

      inspectorBody.innerHTML = '';

      if (events.length === 0) {
        inspectorBody.innerHTML = `<div class="inspector-empty">
          No events captured yet for this subsystem.<br><br>
          Events will appear here as the system processes data.
          Try ingesting training data or sending a prompt.
        </div>`;
        return;
      }

      const countDiv = document.createElement('div');
      countDiv.className = 'inspector-section-title';
      countDiv.textContent = `${events.length} events`;
      inspectorBody.appendChild(countDiv);

      for (const ev of events.slice(0, 80)) {
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = 'inspector-event';
        div.innerHTML = `
          <div class="inspector-event-header">
            <span class="inspector-event-comp">${ev.component}</span>
            <span class="inspector-event-action">${ev.action}</span>
            <span class="inspector-event-ts">${((ev._ts || 0) / 1000).toFixed(1)}s</span>
          </div>
          <div class="inspector-event-data">${formatEventData(ev.data)}</div>
        `;
        div.addEventListener('click', () => showEventDetail(ev));
        inspectorBody.appendChild(div);
      }
    }

    function formatEventData(data) {
      if (!data) return '—';

      const parts = [];

      if (data.stage) parts.push(`stage=${data.stage}`);
      if (data.chunkText) parts.push(`"${data.chunkText.slice(0, 30)}"`);
      if (data.message) parts.push(data.message.slice(0, 40));
      if (data.edgeCount) parts.push(`edges=${data.edgeCount}`);
      if (data.pathCount) parts.push(`paths=${data.pathCount}`);
      if (data.entryCount) parts.push(`entries=${data.entryCount}`);
      if (data.level !== undefined && data.level !== 0) parts.push(`L${data.level}`);
      if (data.bin) parts.push(`bin=${data.bin}`);
      if (data.density) parts.push(`${(data.density * 100).toFixed(0)}%`);
      if (data.preResidue) parts.push(`pre=${data.preResidue}`);
      if (data.postResidue) parts.push(`post=${data.postResidue}`);
      if (data.outcome) parts.push(data.outcome);
      if (data.candidateCount) parts.push(`cand=${data.candidateCount}`);
      if (data.step) parts.push(`step=${data.step}`);

      return parts.join(' · ') || '—';
    }

    // ── State Tab ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    function renderStateTab() {
      inspectorBody.innerHTML = '';

      const components = ZONE_COMPONENTS[inspectorSysKey] || [];
      const events = [];

      for (const comp of components) {
        events.push(...(eventsByComponent.get(comp) || []));
      }

      const section = document.createElement('div');
      section.className = 'inspector-section';

      const title = document.createElement('div');
      title.className = 'inspector-section-title';
      title.textContent = 'Accumulated State';
      section.appendChild(title);

      const stats = computeSubsystemStats(inspectorSysKey, events);

      for (const [key, val] of stats) {
        const row = document.createElement('div');
        row.className = 'inspector-stat';
        row.innerHTML = `<span>${key}</span><span class="val ${val.cls || ''}">${val.text}</span>`;
        section.appendChild(row);
      }

      inspectorBody.appendChild(section);
    }

    function computeSubsystemStats(sysKey, events) {
      const stats = [];

      switch (sysKey) {
        case 'forest': {
          stats.push(['Total Entries', { text: forestEntryCount.toLocaleString() }]);
          stats.push(['Total Inserts', { text: (eventsByComponent.get('LSM') || []).length.toLocaleString() }]);
          const dmtEvents = eventsByComponent.get('DMT') || [];
          stats.push(['DMT Events', { text: dmtEvents.length.toLocaleString() }]);
          const usedBins = forestKeyBins.reduce((c, v) => c + (v > 0 ? 1 : 0), 0);
          stats.push(['Key Prefix Spread', { text: `${usedBins} / 256`, cls: usedBins > 128 ? 'green' : '' }]);
          const totalKeys = forestKeyBins.reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0);
          stats.push(['Total Keys Tracked', { text: totalKeys.toLocaleString() }]);
          break;
        }
        case 'graph': {
          stats.push(['Total Folds', { text: totalFolds.toLocaleString() }]);
          stats.push(['Total Paths', { text: totalPaths.toLocaleString() }]);
          stats.push(['Fold Links', { text: totalFoldLinks.toLocaleString() }]);
          stats.push(['Fold History', { text: foldHistory.length.toLocaleString() }]);
          if (foldHistory.length > 0) {
            const maxLevel = Math.max(...foldHistory.map(f => f.level));
            stats.push(['Max Fold Depth', { text: `L${maxLevel}`, cls: 'accent' }]);
            const avgDensity = foldHistory.reduce((s, f) => s + f.density, 0) / foldHistory.length;
            stats.push(['Avg Fold Density', { text: `${(avgDensity * 100).toFixed(1)}%` }]);
          }
          break;
        }
        case 'machine': {
          stats.push(['Prompts Sent', { text: promptHistory.length.toLocaleString() }]);
          const complete = promptHistory.filter(p => p.stage === 'complete').length;
          const errors = promptHistory.filter(p => p.stage === 'error').length;
          stats.push(['Completed', { text: complete.toLocaleString(), cls: 'green' }]);
          stats.push(['Errors', { text: errors.toLocaleString(), cls: errors > 0 ? 'red' : '' }]);
          stats.push(['Executions', { text: executeHistory.length.toLocaleString() }]);
          const stableCount = executeHistory.filter(e => e.outcome === 'stable').length;
          stats.push(['Stable Outcomes', { text: stableCount.toLocaleString(), cls: 'green' }]);
          break;
        }
        case 'tokenizer': {
          stats.push(['Token Nodes', { text: totalTokenNodes.toLocaleString() }]);
          stats.push(['Ingested Chunks', { text: totalIngested.toLocaleString() }]);
          stats.push(['Queries', { text: totalQueries.toLocaleString() }]);
          const usedBins = tokenBinCounts.reduce((c, v) => c + (v > 0 ? 1 : 0), 0);
          stats.push(['Bin Spread', { text: `${usedBins} / 256` }]);
          break;
        }
        case 'has': {
          const hasEvents = eventsByComponent.get('HAS') || [];
          stats.push(['Events', { text: hasEvents.length.toLocaleString() }]);
          stats.push(['Status', { text: hasEvents.length > 0 ? 'active' : 'awaiting data', cls: hasEvents.length > 0 ? 'green' : '' }]);
          break;
        }
        case 'macroIdx': {
          const macroEvents = eventsByComponent.get('MacroIndex') || [];
          stats.push(['Events', { text: macroEvents.length.toLocaleString() }]);
          stats.push(['Status', { text: macroEvents.length > 0 ? 'active' : 'awaiting data', cls: macroEvents.length > 0 ? 'green' : '' }]);
          break;
        }
        default:
          stats.push(['Total Events', { text: events.length.toLocaleString() }]);
      }

      return stats;
    }

    // ── Internals Tab ─────────────────────────────────────────
    function renderInternalsTab() {
      inspectorBody.innerHTML = '';

      switch (inspectorSysKey) {
        case 'forest': renderForestInternals(); break;
        case 'graph': renderGraphInternals(); break;
        case 'machine': renderMachineInternals(); break;
        case 'tokenizer': renderTokenizerInternals(); break;
        default: renderGenericInternals(); break;
      }
    }

    function renderForestInternals() {
      const sec1 = makeSection('Key Prefix Distribution (256 bins)');

      const totalKeys = forestKeyBins.reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0);
      const maxCount = Math.max(1, ...forestKeyBins);

      if (totalKeys === 0) {
        const emptyMsg = document.createElement('div');
        emptyMsg.className = 'inspector-empty';
        emptyMsg.innerHTML = 'No key data yet. Keys will appear as data is inserted into the radix forest.<br><br>' +
          'Each cell represents a first-byte prefix (0x00–0xFF). Brighter cells have more keys.';
        sec1.appendChild(emptyMsg);
      } else {
        const heatmap = document.createElement('div');
        heatmap.className = 'key-heatmap';

        for (let i = 0; i < 256; i++) {
          const cell = document.createElement('div');
          cell.className = 'heatmap-cell';
          const intensity = forestKeyBins[i] / maxCount;
          cell.style.background = `rgba(140, 200, 255, ${0.05 + intensity * 0.7})`;
          cell.dataset.label = `0x${i.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')}: ${forestKeyBins[i]} keys`;
          heatmap.appendChild(cell);
        }

        sec1.appendChild(heatmap);

        const legend = document.createElement('div');
        legend.className = 'heatmap-legend';
        legend.innerHTML = `<span>0x00</span><span>${totalKeys} total keys</span><span>0xFF</span>`;
        sec1.appendChild(legend);
      }

      inspectorBody.appendChild(sec1);

      const sec2 = makeSection('Recent Insertions');
      const lsmEvents = (eventsByComponent.get('LSM') || []).slice(-20).reverse();

      if (lsmEvents.length === 0) {
        const emptyMsg = document.createElement('div');
        emptyMsg.className = 'inspector-empty';
        emptyMsg.textContent = 'No insertions recorded yet.';
        sec2.appendChild(emptyMsg);
      } else {
        for (const ev of lsmEvents) {
          const row = document.createElement('div');
          row.className = 'fold-tree-node';
          row.innerHTML = `<span class="fold-level">${ev.data?.edgeCount || 0} edges</span> ` +
            `${(ev.data?.chunkText || '').slice(0, 30)}` +
            `<span class="fold-density">${((ev._ts || 0) / 1000).toFixed(1)}s</span>`;
          row.addEventListener('click', () => showEventDetail(ev));
          sec2.appendChild(row);
        }
      }

      inspectorBody.appendChild(sec2);
    }

    function renderGraphInternals() {
      const sec1 = makeSection('Fold Hierarchy');

      if (foldHistory.length === 0) {
        const emptyMsg = document.createElement('div');
        emptyMsg.className = 'inspector-empty';
        emptyMsg.innerHTML = 'No fold events recorded yet.<br><br>' +
          'The fold hierarchy will appear here as the Graph\'s RecursiveFold processes data.';
        sec1.appendChild(emptyMsg);
      } else {
        const container = document.createElement('div');
        container.className = 'fold-tree-container';

        for (const fold of foldHistory.slice(-40).reverse()) {
          const node = document.createElement('div');
          node.className = 'fold-tree-node';
          node.style.marginLeft = `${fold.level * 12}px`;
          node.innerHTML = `<span class="fold-level">L${fold.level}</span> ` +
            `bin=${fold.bin} ch=${fold.children} ` +
            `${fold.text ? `"${fold.text.slice(0, 24)}"` : ''}` +
            `<span class="fold-density">${(fold.density * 100).toFixed(0)}%</span>`;
          container.appendChild(node);
        }

        sec1.appendChild(container);
      }

      inspectorBody.appendChild(sec1);

      const sec2 = makeSection('Fold Density Over Time');
      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
      canvas.width = 360;
      canvas.height = 60;
      canvas.style.width = '100%';
      canvas.style.height = '60px';
      sec2.appendChild(canvas);
      inspectorBody.appendChild(sec2);

      if (foldHistory.length > 1) {
        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        const w = canvas.width, h = canvas.height;
        ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);

        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(64, 128, 192, 0.12)';
        ctx.lineWidth = 1;
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(0, h / 2);
        ctx.lineTo(w, h / 2);
        ctx.stroke();

        const step = w / (foldHistory.length - 1);
        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255, 180, 200, 0.6)';
        ctx.lineWidth = 1;
        ctx.beginPath();

        for (let i = 0; i < foldHistory.length; i++) {
          const x = i * step;
          const y = h - foldHistory[i].density * h;
          if (i === 0) ctx.moveTo(x, y); else ctx.lineTo(x, y);
        }

        ctx.stroke();
      }
    }

    function renderMachineInternals() {
      const sec1 = makeSection('Prompt History');

      if (promptHistory.length === 0) {
        const emptyMsg = document.createElement('div');
        emptyMsg.className = 'inspector-empty';
        emptyMsg.textContent = 'No prompts sent yet. Use the prompt input to query the system.';
        sec1.appendChild(emptyMsg);
      } else {
        for (const p of [...promptHistory].reverse()) {
          const div = document.createElement('div');
          div.className = 'timeline-prompt';
          div.innerHTML = `<div class="prompt-q">Q: ${p.prompt.slice(0, 60)}</div>`;

          if (p.result) {
            div.innerHTML += `<div class="prompt-a">A: ${p.result.slice(0, 80)}</div>`;
          } else if (p.error) {
            div.innerHTML += `<div class="prompt-err">Error: ${p.error.slice(0, 60)}</div>`;
          } else {
            div.innerHTML += `<div style="color:var(--bp-ink-faint);font-size:7px;margin-top:2px">pending…</div>`;
          }

          sec1.appendChild(div);
        }
      }

      inspectorBody.appendChild(sec1);

      const sec2 = makeSection('Execution Traces');

      if (executeHistory.length === 0) {
        const emptyMsg = document.createElement('div');
        emptyMsg.className = 'inspector-empty';
        emptyMsg.textContent = 'No executions recorded yet.';
        sec2.appendChild(emptyMsg);
      } else {
        for (const exec of [...executeHistory].reverse().slice(0, 10)) {
          const div = document.createElement('div');
          div.className = 'timeline-list';

          const header = document.createElement('div');
          header.className = 'timeline-entry';

          const dotCls = exec.outcome === 'stable' ? 'complete'
            : exec.outcome === 'stalled' ? 'error'
            : exec.outcome ? 'pending' : 'active';

          header.innerHTML = `<div class="timeline-dot ${dotCls}"></div>` +
            `<span class="timeline-label">${exec.candidates || 0} candidates</span>` +
            `<span class="timeline-detail">${exec.outcome || 'running'}</span>`;
          div.appendChild(header);

          for (const step of exec.steps.slice(-8)) {
            const stepDiv = document.createElement('div');
            stepDiv.className = 'timeline-entry';
            stepDiv.style.paddingLeft = '18px';
            stepDiv.innerHTML = `<span class="timeline-label" style="font-size:7px">` +
              `step ${step.step}: ${step.pre}→${step.post} ` +
              `${step.stable ? '✓' : step.advanced ? '↓' : '✗'}</span>`;
            div.appendChild(stepDiv);
          }

          sec2.appendChild(div);
        }
      }

      inspectorBody.appendChild(sec2);
    }

    function renderTokenizerInternals() {
      const sec1 = makeSection('Token Bin Distribution');
      const maxVal = Math.max(1, tokenBinMax);
      const usedBins = [];

      for (let i = 0; i < 256; i++) {
        if (tokenBinCounts[i] > 0) usedBins.push(i);
      }

      if (usedBins.length === 0) {
        const emptyMsg = document.createElement('div');
        emptyMsg.className = 'inspector-empty';
        emptyMsg.innerHTML = 'No token bins recorded yet.<br><br>' +
          'Token distribution will appear as data is tokenized.';
        sec1.appendChild(emptyMsg);
      } else {
        const barContainer = document.createElement('div');
        barContainer.className = 'bin-bars';

        for (let i = 0; i < 256; i++) {
          const bar = document.createElement('div');
          bar.className = 'bin-bar';
          const h = (tokenBinCounts[i] / maxVal) * 100;
          bar.style.height = `${Math.max(h, 1)}%`;
          bar.dataset.label = `bin ${i}: ${tokenBinCounts[i]}`;
          barContainer.appendChild(bar);
        }

        sec1.appendChild(barContainer);

        const legend = document.createElement('div');
        legend.className = 'heatmap-legend';
        legend.innerHTML = `<span>bin 0</span><span>${usedBins.length} active bins</span><span>bin 255</span>`;
        sec1.appendChild(legend);
      }

      inspectorBody.appendChild(sec1);

      const sec2 = makeSection('Recent Tokens');
      const tokEvents = (eventsByComponent.get('Tokenizer') || []).slice(-20).reverse();

      if (tokEvents.length === 0) {
        const emptyMsg = document.createElement('div');
        emptyMsg.className = 'inspector-empty';
        emptyMsg.textContent = 'No tokens recorded yet.';
        sec2.appendChild(emptyMsg);
      } else {
        for (const ev of tokEvents) {
          const row = document.createElement('div');
          row.className = 'fold-tree-node';
          row.innerHTML = `<span class="fold-level">bin ${ev.data?.bin || 0}</span> ` +
            `${(ev.data?.chunkText || '').slice(0, 30)}` +
            `<span class="fold-density">${(ev.data?.density * 100 || 0).toFixed(0)}%</span>`;
          row.addEventListener('click', () => showEventDetail(ev));
          sec2.appendChild(row);
        }
      }

      inspectorBody.appendChild(sec2);
    }

    function renderGenericInternals() {
      const emptyMsg = document.createElement('div');
      emptyMsg.className = 'inspector-empty';
      emptyMsg.innerHTML = `This subsystem does not emit telemetry yet.<br><br>
        Once telemetry hooks are added, internal state will be visible here.<br><br>
        <span style="color:var(--bp-accent)">Available data:</span> Check the Feed tab for any events that reference this subsystem.`;
      inspectorBody.appendChild(emptyMsg);
    }

    function makeSection(titleText) {
      const sec = document.createElement('div');
      sec.className = 'inspector-section';
      const t = document.createElement('div');
      t.className = 'inspector-section-title';
      t.textContent = titleText;
      sec.appendChild(t);
      return sec;
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // EVENT DETAIL MODAL
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    function showEventDetail(ev) {
      eventDetailJson.textContent = JSON.stringify(ev, null, 2);
      eventDetailOverlay.style.display = 'flex';
    }

    function closeEventDetail() {
      eventDetailOverlay.style.display = 'none';
    }

    eventDetailCloseBtn.addEventListener('click', closeEventDetail);

    eventDetailOverlay.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      if (e.target === eventDetailOverlay) closeEventDetail();
    });

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // LOG SEARCH / FILTER
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    let logFilterType = 'all';

    const LOG_TYPE_MAP = {
      pipeline: ['pipeline', 'result'],
      ingest: ['ingest'],
      fold: ['fold'],
    };

    function applyLogFilters() {
      const query = (logSearch.value || '').toLowerCase();

      for (const line of logBox.children) {
        const text = line.textContent.toLowerCase();
        const type = line.dataset.type || '';

        let matchFilter = logFilterType === 'all';

        if (!matchFilter && LOG_TYPE_MAP[logFilterType]) {
          matchFilter = LOG_TYPE_MAP[logFilterType].includes(type);
        }

        const matchSearch = !query || text.includes(query);

        line.classList.toggle('filtered-out', !(matchFilter && matchSearch));
      }
    }

    logSearch.addEventListener('input', applyLogFilters);

    document.querySelectorAll('.log-filter-btn').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        logFilterType = btn.dataset.filter;
        document.querySelectorAll('.log-filter-btn').forEach(b =>
          b.classList.toggle('active', b === btn),
        );
        applyLogFilters();
      });
    });

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // KEYBOARD SHORTCUTS
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
      if (e.target.tagName === 'INPUT' || e.target.tagName === 'TEXTAREA') return;

      if (e.key === 'Escape') {
        if (eventDetailOverlay.style.display !== 'none') {
          closeEventDetail();
        } else if (inspectorOpen) {
          closeInspector();
        }
      }

      if (e.key === 'i' || e.key === 'I') {
        if (inspectorOpen) closeInspector();
      }

      const zoneKeys = {
        '1': 'machine',
        '2': 'dataset',
        '3': 'tokenizer',
        '4': 'forest',
        '5': 'graph',
        '6': 'has',
        '7': 'macroIdx',
      };

      if (zoneKeys[e.key]) {
        openInspector(zoneKeys[e.key]);
      }
    });

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // SPARKLINE
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const sparkCanvas = document.getElementById('sparkline-canvas');
    const sparkCtx = sparkCanvas.getContext('2d');
    const sparkData = [];
    const SPARK_MAX = 200;

    function pushSparkDensity(density, action) {
      sparkData.push({ density, action });
      if (sparkData.length > SPARK_MAX) sparkData.shift();
      drawSparkline();
    }

    function drawSparkline() {
      const w = sparkCanvas.width;
      const h = sparkCanvas.height;
      sparkCtx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);

      if (sparkData.length < 2) return;

      sparkCtx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(64, 128, 192, 0.12)';
      sparkCtx.lineWidth = 1;
      sparkCtx.beginPath();
      for (const pct of [0.25, 0.5, 0.75]) {
        const gy = h - pct * h;
        sparkCtx.moveTo(0, gy);
        sparkCtx.lineTo(w, gy);
      }
      sparkCtx.stroke();

      const step = w / (SPARK_MAX - 1);
      sparkCtx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(140, 200, 255, 0.6)';
      sparkCtx.lineWidth = 1;
      sparkCtx.beginPath();
      for (let i = 0; i < sparkData.length; i++) {
        const x = i * step;
        const y = h - sparkData[i].density * h;
        if (i === 0) sparkCtx.moveTo(x, y);
        else sparkCtx.lineTo(x, y);
      }
      sparkCtx.stroke();

      const last = sparkData[sparkData.length - 1];
      sparkCtx.fillStyle = 'rgba(140, 200, 255, 0.5)';
      sparkCtx.font = '7px IBM Plex Mono';
      sparkCtx.fillText(`${(last.density * 257).toFixed(0)}/257`, w - 48, 10);
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // ANIMATION LOOP
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const ZOOM_REF_DIST = 40;
    let prevZoomScale = 1;

    function updateLabelZoom() {
      const dist = camera.position.distanceTo(controls.target);
      const scale = Math.min(Math.max(ZOOM_REF_DIST / dist, 0.8), 4.0);
      const rounded = Math.round(scale * 20) / 20;

      if (rounded !== prevZoomScale) {
        prevZoomScale = rounded;
        labelRenderer.domElement.style.setProperty('--label-zoom', rounded.toFixed(2));
      }
    }

    function animate() {
      requestAnimationFrame(animate);
      updateDataStreams();
      updateLabelZoom();
      controls.update();
      renderer.render(scene, camera);
      labelRenderer.render(scene, camera);
    }

    window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
      camera.aspect = innerWidth / innerHeight;
      camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
      renderer.setSize(innerWidth, innerHeight);
      labelRenderer.setSize(innerWidth, innerHeight);
    });

    animate();
    connect();
  </script>
</body>
</html>
